# The dummy PM is used for buildings that serve no gameplay mechanical purpose but still need to be reacted to be e.g. city hub graphics

pm_dummy = {
	is_default = yes
}

﻿pm_bakery = {
	texture = "gfx/interface/icons/production_method_icons/bakeries.dds"

	building_modifiers = {
		workforce_scaled = {
			# Input goods
			goods_input_grain_add = 40                           # Price:   20, Total cost:   800.0 (100.00%)
			# Output goods
			goods_output_groceries_add = 45                      # Price:   30, Total cost:  1350.0 (100.00%)
			# Total input cost: 800.0
			# Total output cost: 1350.0
			# Profit: 550.0
			# Profit margin: 68.75%
			# Zero profit price multiplier: 0.59
			# Employment: 5000
			# Wage breakeven: 0.11
		}

		level_scaled = {
			# profit = 550
			building_employment_shopkeepers_add = 500
			building_employment_laborers_add = 4500
		}
	}
}

slave_exploitation_sugar = {
	texture = "gfx/interface/icons/production_method_icons/violent_treatment.dds"
	state_modifiers = {
		workforce_scaled = {
			state_slave_import_mult = 0.025
		}
	}

	disallowing_laws = {
		law_slavery_banned
		law_colonial_slavery
		law_debt_slavery ## So India uses other category
	}

	building_modifiers = {
		workforce_scaled = {
			# Input goods
			# Output goods
			goods_output_sugar_add = 50                          # Price:   30, Total cost:  1500.0 (100.00%)
			# Total input cost: 0
			# Total output cost: 1500.0
			# Profit: 1500.0
			# Profit margin: 0.00%
			# Zero profit price multiplier: 0.00
			# Employment: 0
			# Wage breakeven: 0.00
		}

		unscaled = {
			building_laborers_mortality_mult = 0.35
			building_slaves_mortality_mult = 0.35 #sugar is the one slave mortality modifier we kept, for the deadliness 
			building_laborers_job_attractiveness_mult = -0.9 #no one wants to work in sugar as a laborer
			### 1.3-1.4 mortality works out to be around replacement rate (births equal deaths), depending on final SOL of the slave. Historically, sugar slaves were expected to live around 7 years before being replaced, with very few children surviving at all, let alone making adulthood. This mortality level is actually no where near as bad as history, but is much more accurate than previous, and safer for game stability. 
			building_slaves_standard_of_living_add = -3
			building_minimum_wage_mult = -0.15 #you have to pay sugar workers better than other plantations to get them to do this labor
		}
	}
}

			# Zero profit price multiplier: 0.00
			# Employment: 1000
			# Wage breakeven: -7.90
		}

		level_scaled = {
			building_employment_bureaucrats_add = 100
			building_employment_clerks_add = 100
			building_employment_engineers_add = 50
			building_employment_machinists_add = 150
			building_employment_laborers_add = 600
		}
		unscaled = {
			building_laborers_mortality_mult = 0.1
		}
	}

	state_modifiers = {
		workforce_scaled = {
			state_construction_mult = 0.01
		}
	}

	required_input_goods = electricity
}
